{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-sonnet-4-6","id":"msg_01PBbcf7kyDB1tp4onzvJP2y","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01DS5xNZEbsdYhLRxwuwoQHc","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/app/analyze.py","content":"#!/usr/bin/env python3\nimport csv\nimport os\nimport json\nfrom collections import defaultdict\n\n# ── 1. Parse all service reports ────────────────────────────────────────────\nprint(\"Parsing service reports...\")\n\nmaintenance_events = {}  # work_order_id -> {machine_id, technician_id, day, completed_minutes}\n\nwith open('/app/maintenance_work_orders.csv') as f:\n    reader = csv.DictReader(f)\n    for row in reader:\n        wo_id = row['work_order_id']\n        report_path = '/app/' + row['report_path']\n        day = int(row['day'])\n\n        if not os.path.exists(report_path):\n            continue\n\n        with open(report_path) as rf:\n            content = rf.read()\n\n        info = {}\n        for line in content.strip().split('\\n'):\n            if ':' in line:\n                key, val = line.split(':', 1)\n                info[key.strip()] = val.strip()\n\n        machine_id = info.get('MACHINE', '')\n        technician_id = info.get('TECHNICIAN', '')\n        completed_str = info.get('COMPLETED', '')\n\n        # Convert completed time to minutes since midnight\n        if completed_str and ':' in completed_str:\n            h, m = completed_str.split(':')\n            completed_minutes = int(h) * 60 + int(m)\n        else:\n            completed_minutes = 0\n\n        maintenance_events[wo_id] = {\n            'machine_id': machine_id,\n            'technician_id': technician_id,\n            'day': day,\n            'completed_minutes': completed_minutes,\n            'work_order_id': wo_id\n        }\n\nprint(f\"  Loaded {len(maintenance_events)} maintenance events\")\n\n# ── 2. Build machine maintenance timeline ────────────────────────────────────\n# For each machine, sorted list of (day, completed_minutes, work_order_id)\nmachine_maintenance = defaultdict(list)\n\nfor wo_id, evt in maintenance_events.items():\n    machine_id = evt['machine_id']\n    if machine_id:\n        machine_maintenance[machine_id].append((\n            evt['day'],\n            evt['completed_minutes'],\n            wo_id\n        ))\n\n# Sort each machine's events chronologically\nfor machine_id in machine_maintenance:\n    machine_maintenance[machine_id].sort(key=lambda x: (x[0], x[1]))\n\n# ── 3. Parse production batch + machine assignment log ───────────────────────\nprint(\"Parsing production batches and assignments...\")\n\n# batch_id -> {machine_id, product_id, day, start_minutes}\nbatch_info = {}\n\n# From production_batches.csv: batch_id -> {machine_id, product_id, production_day}\nbatch_base = {}\nwith open('/app/production_batches.csv') as f:\n    reader = csv.DictReader(f)\n    for row in reader:\n        batch_base[row['batch_id']] = {\n            'machine_id': row['machine_id'],\n            'product_id': row['product_id'],\n            'production_day': int(row['production_day']),\n            'job_id': row['job_id']\n        }\n\n# From machine_assignment_log.csv: job_id -> {machine_id, day, start_minutes}\njob_assignment = {}\nwith open('/app/machine_assignment_log.csv') as f:\n    reader = csv.DictReader(f)\n    for row in reader:\n        job_id = row['job_id']\n        day = int(row['day'])\n        start_str = row['start_time']\n        h, m = start_str.split(':')\n        start_minutes = int(h) * 60 + int(m)\n        job_assignment[job_id] = {\n            'machine_id': row['machine_id'],\n            'day': day,\n            'start_minutes': start_minutes\n        }\n\n# Merge to get batch_info\nfor batch_id, base in batch_base.items():\n    job_id = base['job_id']\n    assignment = job_assignment.get(job_id)\n    if assignment:\n        batch_info[batch_id] = {\n            'machine_id': base['machine_id'],\n            'product_id': base['product_id'],\n            'day': assignment['day'],\n            'start_minutes': assignment['start_minutes']\n        }\n    else:\n        # Fall back to production_day with no time\n        batch_info[batch_id] = {\n            'machine_id': base['machine_id'],\n            'product_id': base['product_id'],\n            'day': base['production_day'],\n            'start_minutes': 0\n        }\n\nprint(f\"  Loaded {len(batch_info)} batches\")\n\n# ── 4. Parse quality inspections to find rejected batches ────────────────────\nprint(\"Parsing quality inspections...\")\n\nrejected_batches = set()\nwith open('/app/quality_inspections.csv') as f:\n    reader = csv.DictReader(f)\n    for row in reader:\n        if row['inspection_result'] == 'REJECTED':\n            rejected_batches.add(row['batch_id'])\n\nprint(f\"  Found {len(rejected_batches)} rejected batches\")\n\n# ── 5. Link each rejected batch to a maintenance event ──────────────────────\nprint(\"Linking rejected batches to maintenance events...\")\n\n# For a batch on machine M that started at (day, start_min):\n# Find the most recent maintenance on M that completed BEFORE (day, start_min)\n# The next maintenance after that event must start AFTER the batch's production start\n\ndef find_responsible_maintenance(machine_id, prod_day, prod_start_minutes):\n    \"\"\"Return the work_order responsible for the batch, or None.\"\"\"\n    events = machine_maintenance.get(machine_id, [])\n    if not events:\n        return None\n\n    # Convert batch production to a comparable value: (day, start_minutes)\n    batch_time = (prod_day, prod_start_minutes)\n\n    # Find the latest maintenance event completed BEFORE batch production started\n    responsible_idx = None\n    for i, (evt_day, evt_completed_min, wo_id) in enumerate(events):\n        evt_time = (evt_day, evt_completed_min)\n        if evt_time < batch_time:\n            responsible_idx = i\n        else:\n            break\n\n    if responsible_idx is None:\n        return None  # No maintenance before this batch\n\n    # Verify the batch production started before the NEXT maintenance event on same machine\n    next_idx = responsible_idx + 1\n    if next_idx < len(events):\n        next_evt_day, next_evt_completed_min, _ = events[next_idx]\n        # We need to check the START of next maintenance, not completion\n        # But we only have completion time from service reports\n        # The problem says \"production started before the next maintenance event\"\n        # We'll use the next event's completion time as approximation,\n        # but actually we need the start time of the next maintenance.\n        # Since we only have COMPLETED times, let's use those for the next event\n        # as a conservative bound. Actually the condition is production started\n        # before next maintenance EVENT (not its completion).\n        # Let's use completion of next event as upper bound - if production starts\n        # before next completion, that's fine (it's definitely before next event started too\n        # if next_evt_day > prod_day, otherwise we need to check carefully)\n\n        # Actually we should compare production start to next maintenance completion\n        # to be safe. If production started before next maintenance completed,\n        # the batch was likely under the previous maintenance's influence.\n        # But we should use the start of next maintenance ideally.\n        # Since we only have completed times, let's check if prod_day < next_evt_day\n        # OR (prod_day == next_evt_day AND prod_start_minutes < next_evt_completed_min)\n        next_time = (next_evt_day, next_evt_completed_min)\n        if batch_time >= next_time:\n            return None  # Batch produced after next maintenance completed - not under this WO\n\n    return events[responsible_idx][2]  # Return work_order_id\n\n# Map: work_order_id -> set of rejected batch_ids\nwo_to_rejected = defaultdict(set)\n\n# Map: work_order_id -> set of product_ids\nwo_to_products = defaultdict(set)\n\nfor batch_id in rejected_batches:\n    info = batch_info.get(batch_id)\n    if not info:\n        continue\n\n    machine_id = info['machine_id']\n    prod_day = info['day']\n    prod_start_minutes = info['start_minutes']\n    product_id = info['product_id']\n\n    responsible_wo = find_responsible_maintenance(machine_id, prod_day, prod_start_minutes)\n    if responsible_wo:\n        wo_to_rejected[responsible_wo].add(batch_id)\n        wo_to_products[responsible_wo].add(product_id)\n\nprint(f\"  Work orders with linked rejected batches: {len(wo_to_rejected)}\")\n\n# ── 6. Walk through events sorted by (start_day, start_minutes)\n    # Find the latest maintenance that COMPLETED before batch production started\n    responsible_idx = None\n    for i, (evt_day, evt_started_min, evt_completed_min, wo_id) in enumerate(events):\n        # Condition b: maintenance COMPLETED before production started\n        evt_completed_time = (evt_day, evt_completed_min)\n        if evt_completed_time <= batch_time:\n            responsible_idx = i\n\n    if responsible_idx is None:\n        return None  # No maintenance completed before this batch\n\n    # Condition c: production started BEFORE the next maintenance STARTED\n    next_idx = responsible_idx + 1\n    if next_idx < len(events):\n        next_evt_day, next_evt_started_min, _, _ = events[next_idx]\n        next_start_time = (next_evt_day, next_evt_started_min)\n        if batch_time >= next_start_time:\n            return None  # Batch produced after next maintenance started\n\n    return events[responsible_idx][3]  # Return work_order_id\n\nwo_to_rejected = defaultdict(set)\nwo_to_products = defaultdict(set)\n\nfor batch_id in rejected_batches:\n    info = batch_info.get(batch_id)\n    if not info:\n        continue\n\n    machine_id = info['machine_id']\n    prod_day = info['day']\n    prod_start_minutes = info['start_minutes']\n    product_id = info['product_id']\n\n    responsible_wo = find_responsible_maintenance(machine_id, prod_day, prod_start_minutes)\n    if responsible_wo:\n        wo_to_rejected[responsible_wo].add(batch_id)\n        wo_to_products[responsible_wo].add(product_id)\n\nprint(f\"  Work orders with linked rejected batches: {len(wo_to_rejected)}\")\n\n# ── 6. Group by technician ───────────────────────────────────────────────────\nprint(\"Grouping by technician...\")\n\n# technician_id -> list of work orders (each with their batches and products)\ntech_work_orders = defaultdict(list)\n\nfor wo_id, batches in wo_to_rejected.items():\n    evt = maintenance_events.get(wo_id)\n    if not evt:\n        continue\n    tech_id = evt['technician_id']\n    if tech_id:\n        tech_work_orders[tech_id].append({\n            'wo_id': wo_id,\n            'batches': batches,\n            'products': wo_to_products[wo_id]\n        })\n\n# Confirm technicians: >= 3 distinct rejected batches AND >= 2 distinct work orders\nconfirmed_technicians = {}\n\nfor tech_id, wo_list in tech_work_orders.items():\n    total_batches = set()\n    total_products = set()\n    for wo in wo_list:\n        total_batches.update(wo['batches'])\n        total_products.update(wo['products'])\n\n    num_work_orders = len(wo_list)\n    num_batches = len(total_batches)\n\n    if num_batches >= 3 and num_work_orders >= 2:\n        confirmed_technicians[tech_id] = {\n            'work_orders': num_work_orders,\n            'batches': num_batches,\n            'products': total_products\n        }\n        print(f\"  CONFIRMED: {tech_id} | {num_work_orders} WOs | {num_batches} batches | products: {sorted(total_products)}\")\n    else:\n        print(f\"  excluded: {tech_id} | {num_work_orders} WOs | {num_batches} batches\")\n\nprint(f\"\\n  Total confirmed technicians: {len(confirmed_technicians)}\")\n\n# ── 7. Build product -> technicians mapping ──────────────────────────────────\nprint(\"\\nBuilding product -> technicians mapping...\")\n\nproduct_to_techs = defaultdict(set)\n\nfor tech_id, info in confirmed_technicians.items():\n    for product_id in info['products']:\n        product_to_techs[product_id].add(tech_id)\n\nresult = {}\nfor product_id in sorted(product_to_techs.keys()):\n    result[product_id] = sorted(product_to_techs[product_id])\n\nprint(\"\\nFinal result:\")\nprint(json.dumps(result, indent=2))\n\nwith open('/app/answer.json', 'w') as f:\n    json.dump(result, f, indent=2)\n\nprint(\"\\nAnswer written to /app/answer.json\")\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"stop_details":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1436,"cache_read_input_tokens":35300,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":1436,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":49,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"global"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"aed520d5-d122-445d-9a11-7d6e29ba3958","uuid":"b04f4421-ce87-4217-82f1-84cc7e77d1c2","request_id":"req_011CbfCwFNruxKXP2F88kqdY"}

Parse all service reports ────────────────────────────────────────────\nprint(\"Parsing service reports...\")\n\nmaintenance_events = {}  # work_order_id -> {machine_id, technician_id, day, completed_minutes}\n\nwith open('/app/maintenance_work_orders.csv') as f:\n    reader = csv.DictReader(f)\n    for row in reader:\n        wo_id = row['work_order_id']\n        report_path = '/app/' + row['report_path']\n        day = int(row['day'])\n\n        if not os.path.exists(report_path):\n            continue\n\n        with open(report_path) as rf:\n            content = rf.read()\n\n        info = {}\n        for line in content.strip().split('\\n'):\n            if ':' in line:\n                key, val = line.split(':', 1)\n                info[key.strip()] = val.strip()\n\n        machine_id = info.get('MACHINE', '')\n        technician_id = info.get('TECHNICIAN', '')\n        completed_str = info.get('COMPLETED', '')\n\n        # Convert completed time to minutes since midnight\n        if completed_str and ':' in completed_str:\n            h, m = completed_str.split(':')\n            completed_minutes = int(h) * 60 + int(m)\n        else:\n            completed_minutes = 0\n\n        maintenance_events[wo_id] = {\n            'machine_id': machine_id,\n            'technician_id': technician_id,\n            'day': day,\n            'completed_minutes': completed_minutes,\n            'work_order_id': wo_id\n        }\n\nprint(f\"  Loaded {len(maintenance_events)} maintenance events\")\n\n# ── 2. Build machine maintenance timeline ────────────────────────────────────\n# For each machine, sorted list of (day, completed_minutes, work_order_id)\nmachine_maintenance = defaultdict(list)\n\nfor wo_id, evt in maintenance_events.items():\n    machine_id = evt['machine_id']\n    if machine_id:\n        machine_maintenance[machine_id].append((\n            evt['day'],\n            evt['completed_minutes'],\n            wo_id\n        ))\n\n# Sort each machine's events chronologically\nfor machine_id in machine_maintenance:\n    machine_maintenance[machine_id].sort(key=lambda x: (x[0], x[1]))\n\n# ── 3. Parse production batch + machine assignment log ───────────────────────\nprint(\"Parsing production batches and assignments...\")\n\n# batch_id -> {machine_id, product_id, day, start_minutes}\nbatch_info = {}\n\n# From production_batches.csv: batch_id -> {machine_id, product_id, production_day}\nbatch_base = {}\nwith open('/app/production_batches.csv') as f:\n    reader = csv.DictReader(f)\n    for row in reader:\n        batch_base[row['batch_id']] = {\n            'machine_id': row['machine_id'],\n            'product_id': row['product_id'],\n            'production_day': int(row['production_day']),\n            'job_id': row['job_id']\n        }\n\n# From machine_assignment_log.csv: job_id -> {machine_id, day, start_minutes}\njob_assignment = {}\nwith open('/app/machine_assignment_log.csv') as f:\n    reader = csv.DictReader(f)\n    for row in reader:\n        job_id = row['job_id']\n        day = int(row['day'])\n        start_str = row['start_time']\n        h, m = start_str.split(':')\n        start_minutes = int(h) * 60 + int(m)\n        job_assignment[job_id] = {\n            'machine_id': row['machine_id'],\n            'day': day,\n            'start_minutes': start_minutes\n        }\n\n# Merge to get batch_info\nfor batch_id, base in batch_base.items():\n    job_id = base['job_id']\n    assignment = job_assignment.get(job_id)\n    if assignment:\n        batch_info[batch_id] = {\n            'machine_id': base['machine_id'],\n            'product_id': base['product_id'],\n            'day': assignment['day'],\n            'start_minutes': assignment['start_minutes']\n        }\n    else:\n        # Fall back to production_day with no time\n        batch_info[batch_id] = {\n            'machine_id': base['machine_id'],\n            'product_id': base['product_id'],\n            'day': base['production_day'],\n            'start_minutes': 0\n        }\n\nprint(f\"  Loaded {len(batch_info)} batches\")\n\n# ── 4. Parse quality inspections to find rejected batches ────────────────────\nprint(\"Parsing quality inspections...\")\n\nrejected_batches = set()\nwith open('/app/quality_inspections.csv') as f:\n    reader = csv.DictReader(f)\n    for row in reader:\n        if row['inspection_result'] == 'REJECTED':\n            rejected_batches.add(row['batch_id'])\n\nprint(f\"  Found {len(rejected_batches)} rejected batches\")\n\n# ── 5. Link each rejected batch to a maintenance event ──────────────────────\nprint(\"Linking rejected batches to maintenance events...\")\n\n# For a batch on machine M that started at (day, start_min):\n# Find the most recent maintenance on M that completed BEFORE (day, start_min)\n# The next maintenance after that event must start AFTER the batch's production start\n\ndef find_responsible_maintenance(machine_id, prod_day, prod_start_minutes):\n    \"\"\"Return the work_order responsible for the batch, or None.\"\"\"\n    events = machine_maintenance.get(machine_id, [])\n    if not events:\n        return None\n\n    # Convert batch production to a comparable value: (day, start_minutes)\n    batch_time = (prod_day, prod_start_minutes)\n\n    # Find the latest maintenance event completed BEFORE batch production started\n    responsible_idx = None\n    for i, (evt_day, evt_completed_min, wo_id) in enumerate(events):\n        evt_time = (evt_day, evt_completed_min)\n        if evt_time < batch_time:\n            responsible_idx = i\n        else:\n            break\n\n    if responsible_idx is None:\n        return None  # No maintenance before this batch\n\n    # Verify the batch production started before the NEXT maintenance event on same machine\n    next_idx = responsible_idx + 1\n    if next_idx < len(events):\n        next_evt_day, next_evt_completed_min, _ = events[next_idx]\n        # We need to check the START of next maintenance, not completion\n        # But we only have completion time from service reports\n        # The problem says \"production started before the next maintenance event\"\n        # We'll use the next event's completion time as approximation,\n        # but actually we need the start time of the next maintenance.\n        # Since we only have COMPLETED times, let's use those for the next event\n        # as a conservative bound. Actually the condition is production started\n        # before next maintenance EVENT (not its completion).\n        # Let's use completion of next event as upper bound - if production starts\n        # before next completion, that's fine (it's definitely before next event started too\n        # if next_evt_day > prod_day, otherwise we need to check carefully)\n\n        # Actually we should compare production start to next maintenance completion\n        # to be safe. If production started before next maintenance completed,\n        # the batch was likely under the previous maintenance's influence.\n        # But we should use the start of next maintenance ideally.\n        # Since we only have completed times, let's check if prod_day < next_evt_day\n        # OR (prod_day == next_evt_day AND prod_start_minutes < next_evt_completed_min)\n        next_time = (next_evt_day, next_evt_completed_min)\n        if batch_time >= next_time:\n            return None  # Batch produced after next maintenance completed - not under this WO\n\n    return events[responsible_idx][2]  # Return work_order_id\n\n# Map: work_order_id -> set of rejected batch_ids\nwo_to_rejected = defaultdict(set)\n\n# Map: work_order_id -> set of product_ids\nwo_to_products = defaultdict(set)\n\nfor batch_id in rejected_batches:\n    info = batch_info.get(batch_id)\n    if not info:\n        continue\n\n    machine_id = info['machine_id']\n    prod_day = info['day']\n    prod_start_minutes = info['start_minutes']\n    product_id = info['product_id']\n\n    responsible_wo = find_responsible_maintenance(machine_id, prod_day, prod_start_minutes)\n    if responsible_wo:\n        wo_to_rejected[responsible_wo].add(batch_id)\n        wo_to_products[responsible_wo].add(product_id)\n\nprint(f\"  Work orders with linked rejected batches: {len(wo_to_rejected)}\")\n\n# ── 6. Group by technician ───────────────────────────────────────────────────\nprint(\"Grouping by technician...\")\n\n# technician_id -> list of (work_order_id, set of rejected batch_ids, set of products)\ntech_work_orders = defaultdict(list)\n\nfor wo_id, batches in wo_to_rejected.items():\n    evt = maintenance_events.get(wo_id)\n    if not evt:\n        continue\n    tech_id = evt['technician_id']\n    if tech_id:\n        tech_work_orders[tech_id].append({\n            'wo_id': wo_id,\n            'batches': batches,\n            'products': wo_to_products[wo_id]\n        })\n\n# Confirm technicians: >= 3 distinct rejected batches AND >= 2 distinct work orders\nconfirmed_technicians = {}\n\nfor tech_id, wo_list in tech_work_orders.items():\n    total_batches = set()\n    total_products = set()\n    for wo in wo_list:\n        total_batches.update(wo['batches'])\n        total_products.update(wo['products'])\n\n    num_work_orders = len(wo_list)\n    num_batches = len(total_batches)\n\n    if num_batches >= 3 and num_work_orders >= 2:\n        confirmed_technicians[tech_id] = {\n            'work_orders': num_work_orders,\n            'batches': num_batches,\n            'products': total_products\n        }\n        print(f\"  CONFIRMED: {tech_id} | {num_work_orders} WOs | {num_batches} rejected batches | products: {sorted(total_products)}\")\n\nprint(f\"\\n  Total confirmed technicians: {len(confirmed_technicians)}\")\n\n# ── 7. Build product -> technicians mapping ──────────────────────────────────\nprint(\"\\nBuilding product -> technicians mapping...\")\n\nproduct_to_techs = defaultdict(set)\n\nfor tech_id, info in confirmed_technicians.items():\n    for product_id in info['products']:\n        product_to_techs[product_id].add(tech_id)\n\n# Sort and format\nresult = {}\nfor product_id in sorted(product_to_techs.keys()):\n    result[product_id] = sorted(product_to_techs[product_id])\n\nprint(\"\\nFinal result:\")\nprint(json.dumps(result, indent=2))\n\n# Write to answer.json\nwith open('/app/answer.json', 'w') as f:\n    json.dump(result, f, indent=2)\n\nprint(\"\\nAnswer written to /app/answer.json\")\n","userModified":false}}
